### FRENCH
### By Xavier Zimmermann

# Principes :
# L'écriture de la commande: Get + chaîne au masculin avec majuscule + chaîne au féminin avec majuscule
# Ajouter Cap à la fin pour avoir une majuscule dans le texte cible
# Ajouter Opp pour inverser le masculin et le féminin
# L'apostrophe pour les élisions n'est pas représenté dans le nom des commandes
# Le paramètre "fallback_text" permet d'avoir une ligne de localisation utilisée au cas où aucune condition n'est remplie, en l'occurrence la commande anglaise correspondante.

## COMMANDE ACCOLEE A UNE COMMANDE OU UN MOT (PAS D'ESPACE ENTRE LES DEUX)
# Get_only_du_RealmFull (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_en_RealmFull (dans le\dans la\dans l'\chez les devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_le_RealmFull (le\la\l'\les devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_au_RealmFull (AuAlaAux devant GetFullName dans un scope de titre ou GetFullBaseName) *TITLE
# Get_only_du_Realm (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetName) *TITLE
# Get_only_le_Realm (le\la\l'\les devant GetName) *TITLE
# Get_only_en_Realm (en\dans le\dans la\dans l'\dans les\chez les devant GetName) *TITLE
# Get_only_du_Title (du\de la\de l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_le_Title (le\la\l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_Le_Title (Le\La\L' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_au_Title (au\à la\à l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_Au_Title (Au\À la\À l' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_e_Title (e\' devant GetTitledFirstNameNoRegnal|GetTitledFirstName|GetTitledFirstNameWithNick|GetTitledName|GetTitle|GetBestName|GetTitledNameWithNick|GetLawProposer|GetRulerTitle) *TITLE
# Get_only_du_Society (du\de la\de l'\des devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_le_Society (le\la\l'\les devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_Le_Society (Le\La\L'\Les devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_au_Society (au\à la\à l'\aux devant Society.GetName) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_le_SocietyRank (le\la\l' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_Le_SocietyRank (Le\La\L' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_au_SocietyRank (au\à la\à l'\aux devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_du_SocietyRank (du\de la\de l' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_e_SocietyRank (e\' devant GetSocietyRank) *SOCIETY
# Get_only_le_JobTitle (le\la\l' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_Le_JobTitle (Le\La\L' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_du_JobTitle (du\de la\de l' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_au_JobTitle (au\à la\à l' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_on_JobTitle (on\a devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_e_JobTitle (e\' devant GetJobTitle) *JOB TITLE
# Get_only_du_SelectedIngredient_1 (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_du_SelectedIngredient_2 (du\de la\de l'\des devant GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_le_SelectedIngredient_1 (le\la\l'\les devant GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_le_SelectedIngredient_2 (le\la\l'\les devant GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_e_SelectedIngredient_1 (e\' devant GetSelectedIngredient_1) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_e_SelectedIngredient_2 (e\' devant GetSelectedIngredient_2) *INGREDIENT
# Get_only_du_HighGod (du\de la\de l' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_au_HighGod (au\à la\à l' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_le_HighGod (le\la\l' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_Le_HighGod (Le\La\L' devant Religion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_du_HighGodTrue (du\de la\de l' devant TrueReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_au_HighGodTrue (au\à la\à l' devant TrueReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_le_HighGodTrue (le\la\l' devant TrueReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_du_HighGodSecret (du\de la\de l' devant SecretReligion.GetHighGodName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_le_Scripture (le\la\l'\les devant Religion.GetScriptureName) *RELIGION
# Get_only_du_Scripture (du\de la\de l'\des devant Religion.GetScriptureName) *RELIGION

defined_text = {
	name = GetIlElle
	use_first_valid = yes

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetIlElle_male
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_GetIlElle_female
	}
}

defined_text = {
	name = Get_E
	use_first_valid = yes

	text = {
		localisation_key = "" # N'affiche rien
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}

						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

						OR = {
							culture_group = altaic # Khaganat
							culture = russian # Tsarat
						}
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = KING } # Royaume, Khanat, Sultanat
						NOT = { culture = saxon } # Grande chefferie
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Raj
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Raj
							culture = norse # Jarldómr
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						tier = COUNT

						OR = {
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Thikana
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Thikana
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						OR = {
							religion_group = muslim # Califat
							religion = orthodox # Patriarcat
						}
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
						religion_group = muslim # Cheikat
					}
					trigger_else = {
						tier = BARON # Temple, Vahram, Khalwat

						NOR = {
							religion_group = christian # Évêché
							religion_group = muslim # Mosquée
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					is_nomadic = yes # Khaganat, Khanat
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {

					trigger_else = {
						real_tier = BARON # Baronnie

						NOR = {
							culture = mongol # Taïshi
							culture = turkish # Timar
							culture_group = iranian # Arg
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { is_tribal = yes }

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = KING }
						culture = saxon # Grande chefferie
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE } # Grande chefferie

						NOR = {
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Raj
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Raj
							culture = norse # Jarldómr
						}
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT } # Chefferie

						NOR = {
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Thikana
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Thikana
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						real_tier = BARON # Tribu, Dama
					}
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						NOR = {
							religion = catholic # Théocratie
							religion_group = pagan_group # Théocratie
						}
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							religion_group = muslim # Théocratie
							religion_group = pagan_group # Théocratie
						}
					}
					trigger_else_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }
						religion_group = pagan_group # Théocratie
					}
					trigger_else = {
						real_tier = BARON
						religion_group = muslim # Mosquée
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					is_republic = yes # Cité, Grande cité, République, Principauté, République Sérénissime, Ligue marchande, Ligue
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_l
		trigger = {
			holder_scope = {
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_feudal = yes }

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

						NOR = {
							culture_group = altaic # Khaganat
							culture = russian # Tsarat
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						real_tier = DUKE
						culture_group = arabic # Émirat
					}
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { is_tribal = yes }

					real_tier = EMPEROR

					NOR = {
						culture_group = altaic # Khaganat
						culture = russian # Tsarat
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					is_theocracy = yes
					lower_real_tier_than = KING # Archevêché princier, Évêché princier, Évêché
					religion_group = christian
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_ACCENT
	}

defined_text = { # 2018.10.30
	name = Get_only_du_Title
	use_first_valid = yes

	text = { # Titre temporaire non nommé (en révolte, aventurier, ordre sacré)
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_
		trigger = {
			primary_title = { temporary = yes }
		}
	}
	text = { # titres honorifiques
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = {
			# Prince, Rajkumar, Shahzada, César
			has_minor_title = title_prince
			is_female = no
			lower_real_tier_than = KING
			prisoner = no

			NOR = {
				# non si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
				spouse = {
					lower_real_tier_than = KING
					primary_title = { temporary = no }
				}

				trait = bastard # non si bâtard
			}
		}
	}
	text = { # titres honorifiques
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_la_
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = { # Kaiserin
				limit = { has_minor_title = title_queen_mother }
				culture = german
			}
			trigger_else = { # Princesse, Rajkumari, Shahdokht, Caesarina
				has_minor_title = title_prince
				is_female = yes
				lower_real_tier_than = KING
				prisoner = no

				NOR = {
					# non si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
					spouse = {
						higher_real_tier_than = DUKE
						primary_title = { temporary = no }
					}

					trait = bastard # non si bâtard
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = { # titres honorifiques
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_l
		trigger = {
			has_minor_title = title_queen_mother # Impératrice douairière
			NOT = { culture = german } # Kaiseri
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = { # homme qui contrôle une religion
			controls_religion = yes
			is_female = no
		}
	}

		localisation_key = String_FR_de_la_
		trigger = { # femme qui contrôle une religion
			controls_religion = yes
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = { # homme avec un titre spécial
			is_female = no

			primary_title = {
				OR = {
					# title = e_sunni # CALIPH Calife
					# title = e_shiite # CALIPH Calife

					title = d_sunni_cuman_company # CAPTAIN Capitaine
					title = d_sunni_berber_company # CAPTAIN Capitaine

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_l
		trigger = { # homme avec un titre spécial
			is_female = no

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_la_
		trigger = { # femme avec un titre spécial
			is_female = yes

			primary_title = {

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_
		trigger = { # Doit être après les titres spéciaux. Pour les "Bande [culture]". Le capitaine n'a pas de titre nommé
			mercenary = yes
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_landed = yes }

				OR = {
					AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...
						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse } # le conjoint n'a pas un titre non temporaire supérieur

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}

					spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron

						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # N'a aucun titre foncier et l'éventuel conjoint non plus
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_married = yes }
					spouse = { is_landed = no }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_feudal = yes } # gouvernements féodaux

				OR = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR } # Empereur, Impératrice

						NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
							culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
							culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
							culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
							culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
							culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
							culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
							culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

							trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
								limit = { is_female = no }

								OR = {
									culture = turkish # Padishah
									culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
									culture_group = arabic # Badshah
								}
							}
						}
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
						spouse = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice

							NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
								culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
								culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
								culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
								culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
								culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
								culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
								culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

								trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
									limit = { is_female = yes }

									OR = {
										culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
										culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										culture = turkish # Padishah
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Exarque
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						culture_group = byzantine

						primary_title = {
							is_vice_royalty = yes
						}

						# conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Exarque)
						lower_real_tier_than = KING

						spouse = {
							real_tier = KING

							primary_title = {
								is_vice_royalty = yes
							}

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = byzantine
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = byzantine
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

							liege = {
								culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira
							}

							trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
								limit = { is_female = no }
								culture = sogdian
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE

						spouse = {
							real_tier = DUKE

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

									trigger_if = {
										limit = { is_female = yes }
										culture = sogdian # Ikhshide
									}
									trigger_else = {
										culture_group = iranian # Émira
									}
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

										trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
											limit = {
												PREV = { is_female = yes }
											}

											culture = sogdian
										}
										trigger_else = { # Émira
											culture_group = iranian
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Earl
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

						is_female = no

						OR = {
							culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
							culture = english # Earl
							culture = scottish # Earl
							culture = irish # Earl
							culture = pictish # Earl
						}

						liege = {
							OR = {
								culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}

					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Earl)
						lower_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = COUNT

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture = anglo-saxon
									culture = english
									culture = scottish
									culture = irish
									culture = pictish
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = anglo-saxon
										culture = english
										culture = scottish
										culture = irish
										culture = pictish
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = BARON }

						is_female = no
						culture_group = iranian # Argbadh

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
						lower_real_tier_than = BARON
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = BARON

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = iranian
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = iranian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements théocratiques
				limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					religion_group = pagan_group
					is_female = yes
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					religion_group = pagan_group
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Ayatollah
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

					religion = shiite
					is_female = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					real_tier = BARON

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = christian } # Évêque

						NOR = {
							has_minor_title = title_cardinal
							has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						religion = zoroastrian # Ervad
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements tribaux
				limit = { is_tribal = yes }

				primary_title = {
					temporary = no
				}

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					is_female = yes

					NOR = { # sauf quand:
						culture_group = altaic
						culture_group = dravidian_group
						culture_group = indo_aryan_group
						culture = russian
					}
				}

				trigger_else = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
					spouse = {
						real_tier = EMPEROR
						is_female = no

						NOR = { # sauf quand:
							culture_group = altaic
							culture_group = dravidian_group
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group
							culture = russian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_du_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_de_la_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

	text = {
		localisation_key = ""
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_landed = yes }

				OR = {
					AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...
						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse } # le conjoint n'a pas un titre non temporaire supérieur

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}

					spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron

						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # N'a aucun titre foncier et l'éventuel conjoint non plus
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_married = yes }
					spouse = { is_landed = no }
				}
			}
		}

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_feudal = yes } # gouvernements féodaux

				OR = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR } # Empereur, Impératrice

						NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
							culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
							culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
							culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
							culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
							culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
							culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
							culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

							trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
								limit = { is_female = no }

								OR = {
									culture = turkish # Padishah
									culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
									culture_group = arabic # Badshah
								}
							}
						}
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
						spouse = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice

							NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
								culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
								culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
								culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
								culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
								culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
								culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
								culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

								trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
									limit = { is_female = yes }

									OR = {
										culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
										culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										culture = turkish # Padishah
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Exarque
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						culture_group = byzantine

						primary_title = {
							is_vice_royalty = yes
						}

						# conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Exarque)
						lower_real_tier_than = KING

						spouse = {
							real_tier = KING

							primary_title = {
								is_vice_royalty = yes
							}

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = byzantine
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = byzantine
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

							liege = {
								culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira
							}

							trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
								limit = { is_female = no }
								culture = sogdian
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE

						spouse = {
							real_tier = DUKE

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

									trigger_if = {
										limit = { is_female = yes }
										culture = sogdian # Ikhshide
									}
									trigger_else = {
										culture_group = iranian # Émira
									}
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

										trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
											limit = {
												PREV = { is_female = yes }
											}

											culture = sogdian
										}
										trigger_else = { # Émira
											culture_group = iranian
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Earl
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

						is_female = no

						OR = {
							culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
							culture = english # Earl
							culture = scottish # Earl
							culture = irish # Earl
							culture = pictish # Earl
						}

						liege = {
							OR = {
								culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}

					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Earl)
						lower_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = COUNT

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture = anglo-saxon
									culture = english
									culture = scottish
									culture = irish
									culture = pictish
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = anglo-saxon
										culture = english
										culture = scottish
										culture = irish
										culture = pictish
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = BARON }

						is_female = no
						culture_group = iranian # Argbadh

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
						lower_real_tier_than = BARON
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = BARON

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = iranian
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = iranian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements théocratiques
				limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					religion_group = pagan_group
					is_female = yes
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					religion_group = pagan_group
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Ayatollah
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

					religion = shiite
					is_female = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					real_tier = BARON

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = christian } # Évêque

						NOR = {
							has_minor_title = title_cardinal
							has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						religion = zoroastrian # Ervad
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements tribaux
				limit = { is_tribal = yes }

				primary_title = {
					temporary = no
				}

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					is_female = yes

					NOR = { # sauf quand:
						culture_group = altaic
						culture_group = dravidian_group
						culture_group = indo_aryan_group
						culture = russian
					}
				}

				trigger_else = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
					spouse = {
						real_tier = EMPEROR
						is_female = no

						NOR = { # sauf quand:
							culture_group = altaic
							culture_group = dravidian_group
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group
							culture = russian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_le_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_la_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

	text = {
		localisation_key = ""
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_landed = yes }

				OR = {
					AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...
						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse } # le conjoint n'a pas un titre non temporaire supérieur

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}

					spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron

						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # N'a aucun titre foncier et l'éventuel conjoint non plus
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_married = yes }
					spouse = { is_landed = no }
				}
			}
		}

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_L
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_feudal = yes } # gouvernements féodaux

				OR = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR } # Empereur, Impératrice

						NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
							culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
							culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
							culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
							culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
							culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
							culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
							culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

							trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
								limit = { is_female = no }

								OR = {
									culture = turkish # Padishah
									culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
									culture_group = arabic # Badshah
								}
							}
						}
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
						spouse = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice

							NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
								culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
								culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
								culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
								culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
								culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
								culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
								culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

								trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
									limit = { is_female = yes }

									OR = {
										culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
										culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										culture = turkish # Padishah
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Exarque
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						culture_group = byzantine

						primary_title = {
							is_vice_royalty = yes
						}

						# conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Exarque)
						lower_real_tier_than = KING

						spouse = {
							real_tier = KING

							primary_title = {
								is_vice_royalty = yes
							}

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = byzantine
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = byzantine
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

							liege = {
								culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira
							}

							trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
								limit = { is_female = no }
								culture = sogdian
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE

						spouse = {
							real_tier = DUKE

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

									trigger_if = {
										limit = { is_female = yes }
										culture = sogdian # Ikhshide
									}
									trigger_else = {
										culture_group = iranian # Émira
									}
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

										trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
											limit = {
												PREV = { is_female = yes }
											}

											culture = sogdian
										}
										trigger_else = { # Émira
											culture_group = iranian
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Earl
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

						is_female = no

						OR = {
							culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
							culture = english # Earl
							culture = scottish # Earl
							culture = irish # Earl
							culture = pictish # Earl
						}

						liege = {
							OR = {
								culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}

					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Earl)
						lower_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = COUNT

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture = anglo-saxon
									culture = english
									culture = scottish
									culture = irish
									culture = pictish
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = anglo-saxon
										culture = english
										culture = scottish
										culture = irish
										culture = pictish
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = BARON }

						is_female = no
						culture_group = iranian # Argbadh

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
						lower_real_tier_than = BARON
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = BARON

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = iranian
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = iranian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements théocratiques
				limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					religion_group = pagan_group
					is_female = yes
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					religion_group = pagan_group
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Ayatollah
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

					religion = shiite
					is_female = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					real_tier = BARON

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = christian } # Évêque

						NOR = {
							has_minor_title = title_cardinal
							has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						religion = zoroastrian # Ervad
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements tribaux
				limit = { is_tribal = yes }

				primary_title = {
					temporary = no
				}

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					is_female = yes

					NOR = { # sauf quand:
						culture_group = altaic
						culture_group = dravidian_group
						culture_group = indo_aryan_group
						culture = russian
					}
				}

				trigger_else = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
					spouse = {
						real_tier = EMPEROR
						is_female = no

						NOR = { # sauf quand:
							culture_group = altaic
							culture_group = dravidian_group
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group
							culture = russian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_Le_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_La_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

	text = {

	text = {
		trigger = { # Doit être après les titres spéciaux. Pour les "Bande [culture]". Le capitaine n'a pas de titre nommé
			mercenary = yes
		}
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_ACCENT
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_ACCENT
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_landed = yes }

				OR = {
					AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...
						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse } # le conjoint n'a pas un titre non temporaire supérieur

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}

					spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron

						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # N'a aucun titre foncier et l'éventuel conjoint non plus
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_married = yes }
					spouse = { is_landed = no }
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_feudal = yes } # gouvernements féodaux

				OR = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR } # Empereur, Impératrice

						NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
							culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
							culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
							culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
							culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
							culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
							culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
							culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

							trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
								limit = { is_female = no }

								OR = {
									culture = turkish # Padishah
									culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
									culture_group = arabic # Badshah
								}
							}
						}
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
						spouse = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice

							NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
								culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
								culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
								culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
								culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
								culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
								culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
								culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

								trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
									limit = { is_female = yes }

									OR = {
										culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
										culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										culture = turkish # Padishah
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Exarque
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						culture_group = byzantine

						primary_title = {
							is_vice_royalty = yes
						}

						# conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Exarque)
						lower_real_tier_than = KING

						spouse = {
							real_tier = KING

							primary_title = {
								is_vice_royalty = yes
							}

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = byzantine
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = byzantine
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

							liege = {
								culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira
							}

							trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
								limit = { is_female = no }
								culture = sogdian
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE

						spouse = {
							real_tier = DUKE

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

									trigger_if = {
										limit = { is_female = yes }
										culture = sogdian # Ikhshide
									}
									trigger_else = {
										culture_group = iranian # Émira
									}
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

										trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
											limit = {
												PREV = { is_female = yes }
											}

											culture = sogdian
										}
										trigger_else = { # Émira
											culture_group = iranian
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Earl
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

						is_female = no

						OR = {
							culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
							culture = english # Earl
							culture = scottish # Earl
							culture = irish # Earl
							culture = pictish # Earl
						}

						liege = {
							OR = {
								culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}

					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Earl)
						lower_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = COUNT

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture = anglo-saxon
									culture = english
									culture = scottish
									culture = irish
									culture = pictish
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = anglo-saxon
										culture = english
										culture = scottish
										culture = irish
										culture = pictish
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = BARON }

						is_female = no
						culture_group = iranian # Argbadh

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
						lower_real_tier_than = BARON
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = BARON

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = iranian
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = iranian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements théocratiques
				limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					religion_group = pagan_group
					is_female = yes
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					religion_group = pagan_group
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Ayatollah
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

					religion = shiite
					is_female = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					real_tier = BARON

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = christian } # Évêque

						NOR = {
							has_minor_title = title_cardinal
							has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						religion = zoroastrian # Ervad
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements tribaux
				limit = { is_tribal = yes }

				primary_title = {
					temporary = no
				}

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					is_female = yes

					NOR = { # sauf quand:
						culture_group = altaic
						culture_group = dravidian_group
						culture_group = indo_aryan_group
						culture = russian
					}
				}

				trigger_else = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
					spouse = {
						real_tier = EMPEROR
						is_female = no

						NOR = { # sauf quand:
							culture_group = altaic
							culture_group = dravidian_group
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group
							culture = russian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_au_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_a_la_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

					}

			primary_title = {

					# title = e_sunni # CALIPH Calife
					# title = e_shiite # CALIPH Calife

			mercenary = yes

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_A_ACCENT
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_landed = yes }

				OR = {
					AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...
						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse } # le conjoint n'a pas un titre non temporaire supérieur

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}

					spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron

						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # N'a aucun titre foncier et l'éventuel conjoint non plus
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_married = yes }
					spouse = { is_landed = no }
				}
			}
		}

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_A_l
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_feudal = yes } # gouvernements féodaux

				OR = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR } # Empereur, Impératrice

						NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
							culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
							culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
							culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
							culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
							culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
							culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
							culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

							trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
								limit = { is_female = no }

								OR = {
									culture = turkish # Padishah
									culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
									culture_group = arabic # Badshah
								}
							}
						}
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
						spouse = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice

							NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
								culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
								culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
								culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
								culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
								culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
								culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
								culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

								trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
									limit = { is_female = yes }

									OR = {
										culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
										culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										culture = turkish # Padishah
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Exarque
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						culture_group = byzantine

						primary_title = {
							is_vice_royalty = yes
						}

						# conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Exarque)
						lower_real_tier_than = KING

						spouse = {
							real_tier = KING

							primary_title = {
								is_vice_royalty = yes
							}

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = byzantine
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = byzantine
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

							liege = {
								culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira
							}

							trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
								limit = { is_female = no }
								culture = sogdian
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE

						spouse = {
							real_tier = DUKE

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

									trigger_if = {
										limit = { is_female = yes }
										culture = sogdian # Ikhshide
									}
									trigger_else = {
										culture_group = iranian # Émira
									}
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

										trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
											limit = {
												PREV = { is_female = yes }
											}

											culture = sogdian
										}
										trigger_else = { # Émira
											culture_group = iranian
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Earl
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

						is_female = no

						OR = {
							culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
							culture = english # Earl
							culture = scottish # Earl
							culture = irish # Earl
							culture = pictish # Earl
						}

						liege = {
							OR = {
								culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}

					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Earl)
						lower_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = COUNT

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture = anglo-saxon
									culture = english
									culture = scottish
									culture = irish
									culture = pictish
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = anglo-saxon
										culture = english
										culture = scottish
										culture = irish
										culture = pictish
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = BARON }

						is_female = no
						culture_group = iranian # Argbadh

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
						lower_real_tier_than = BARON
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = BARON

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = iranian
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = iranian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements théocratiques
				limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					religion_group = pagan_group
					is_female = yes
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					religion_group = pagan_group
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Ayatollah
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

					religion = shiite
					is_female = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					real_tier = BARON

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = christian } # Évêque

						NOR = {
							has_minor_title = title_cardinal
							has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						religion = zoroastrian # Ervad
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements tribaux
				limit = { is_tribal = yes }

				primary_title = {
					temporary = no
				}

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					is_female = yes

					NOR = { # sauf quand:
						culture_group = altaic
						culture_group = dravidian_group
						culture_group = indo_aryan_group
						culture = russian
					}
				}

				trigger_else = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
					spouse = {
						real_tier = EMPEROR
						is_female = no

						NOR = { # sauf quand:
							culture_group = altaic
							culture_group = dravidian_group
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group
							culture = russian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_Au_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_A_la_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_landed = yes }

				OR = {
					AND = { # cultures pour lesquelles le titre n'est pas nommé...
						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse } # le conjoint n'a pas un titre non temporaire supérieur

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}

					spouse = { #... et n'est donc pas donné au conjoint
						higher_real_tier_than = spouse # le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE # rang comte ou baron

						OR = { # gouvernement féodal ou tribal
							is_feudal = yes
							is_tribal = yes
						}

						OR = { # culture
							culture = bodpa
							culture = frisian
							culture = nepali
							culture = norse
							culture = saxon
							culture = sumpa
							culture = tangut
							culture = zhangzhung
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # N'a aucun titre foncier et l'éventuel conjoint non plus
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { is_married = yes }
					spouse = { is_landed = no }
				}
			}
		}

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_APOSTROPHE
		trigger = { # titres qui commencent par une voyelle
			trigger_if = {
				limit = { is_feudal = yes } # gouvernements féodaux

				OR = {
					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR } # Empereur, Impératrice

						NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
							culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
							culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
							culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
							culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
							culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
							culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
							culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
							culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
							culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

							trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
								limit = { is_female = no }

								OR = {
									culture = turkish # Padishah
									culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
									culture_group = arabic # Badshah
								}
							}
						}
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint féodal donne le titre (si rang inférieur)
						spouse = {
							real_tier = EMPEROR # Empereur, Impératrice

							NOR = { # Titres d'empereurs et d'impératrices féodaux commençant par une consonne
								culture_group = dravidian_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = indo_aryan_group # Samrat, Samrajni
								culture_group = altaic # Khagan, Khatoun
								culture_group = tibetan_group # Tsenpo, Tsenmo
								culture = german # Kaiser, Kaiserin
								culture = greek # Basileus, Basilissa
								culture = tangut # Thu Ghu, Thu Ghu
								culture = nepali # Maharani, Samrata
								culture = russian # Tsar, Tsarine
								culture = nahua # Huetlatoani, Huetlatoani

								trigger_if = { # Titres d'empereurs féodaux commençant par une consonne
									limit = { is_female = yes }

									OR = {
										culture_group = iranian # Shahanshah
										culture_group = arabic # Badshah
										culture = turkish # Padishah
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Exarque
						limit = { real_tier = KING }

						culture_group = byzantine

						primary_title = {
							is_vice_royalty = yes
						}

						# conjoint de rang empereur avec un titre non temporaire
						NOT = { lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Exarque)
						lower_real_tier_than = KING

						spouse = {
							real_tier = KING

							primary_title = {
								is_vice_royalty = yes
							}

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = byzantine
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = byzantine
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = DUKE }

						OR = {
							culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

							liege = {
								culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira
							}

							trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
								limit = { is_female = no }
								culture = sogdian
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à duc
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Émir Émira Ikhshide)
						lower_real_tier_than = DUKE

						spouse = {
							real_tier = DUKE

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

									trigger_if = {
										limit = { is_female = yes }
										culture = sogdian # Ikhshide
									}
									trigger_else = {
										culture_group = iranian # Émira
									}
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture_group = arabic # Émir Émira

										trigger_if = { # Ikhshide
											limit = {
												PREV = { is_female = yes }
											}

											culture = sogdian
										}
										trigger_else = { # Émira
											culture_group = iranian
										}
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = { # Earl
						limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

						is_female = no

						OR = {
							culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
							culture = english # Earl
							culture = scottish # Earl
							culture = irish # Earl
							culture = pictish # Earl
						}

						liege = {
							OR = {
								culture = anglo-saxon # Earl
								culture = english # Earl
								culture = scottish # Earl
								culture = irish # Earl
								culture = pictish # Earl
							}
						}

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à comte
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}

					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Earl)
						lower_real_tier_than = COUNT
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = COUNT

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }

								OR = {
									culture = anglo-saxon
									culture = english
									culture = scottish
									culture = irish
									culture = pictish
								}
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									OR = {
										culture = anglo-saxon
										culture = english
										culture = scottish
										culture = irish
										culture = pictish
									}
								}
							}
						}
					}

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { real_tier = BARON }

						is_female = no
						culture_group = iranian # Argbadh

						# si le conjoint a un titre non temporaire supérieur à baron
						NOT = {	lower_real_tier_than = spouse }
					}
					trigger_else = { # conjoint (Argbadh)
						lower_real_tier_than = BARON
						is_female = no

						spouse = {
							real_tier = BARON

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { independent = yes }
								culture_group = iranian
							}
							trigger_else = {
								liege = {
									culture_group = iranian
								}
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements théocratiques
				limit = { is_theocracy = yes }

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					religion_group = pagan_group
					is_female = yes
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Archiprêtre, Archiprêtresse
					limit = { real_tier = DUKE }
					religion_group = pagan_group
				}
				trigger_else_if = { # Ayatollah
					limit = { real_tier = COUNT }

					religion = shiite
					is_female = no
				}
				trigger_else = {
					real_tier = BARON

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = christian } # Évêque

						NOR = {
							has_minor_title = title_cardinal
							has_minor_title = title_fraticelli_cardinal
						}
					}
					trigger_else = {
						religion = zoroastrian # Ervad
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = { # gouvernements tribaux
				limit = { is_tribal = yes }

				primary_title = {
					temporary = no
				}

				trigger_if = { # Impératrice (femme tribale rang empereur non temporaire)
					limit = { real_tier = EMPEROR }

					is_female = yes

					NOR = { # sauf quand:
						culture_group = altaic
						culture_group = dravidian_group
						culture_group = indo_aryan_group
						culture = russian
					}
				}

				trigger_else = { # conjoint empereur tribal non temporaire donne son titre
					spouse = {
						real_tier = EMPEROR
						is_female = no

						NOR = { # sauf quand:
							culture_group = altaic
							culture_group = dravidian_group
							culture_group = indo_aryan_group
							culture = russian
						}
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_nickname = nick_the_elder # Ancien
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}

		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}

defined_text = {
	name = Get_only_le_SocietyRank
	use_first_valid = yes

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_l
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = secret_religious_cult
						society_member_of = monastic_order_benedictine
						society_member_of = monastic_order_dominican
					}
				}

				society_rank == 2
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { society_member_of = hermetics }

				OR = {
					society_rank == 2
					society_rank == 3
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { society_member_of = monastic_order_buddhist }
				society_rank >= 3
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_hindu
						society_member_of = monastic_order_jain
					}
				}

				society_rank == 4
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_monophysite
						society_member_of = monastic_order_nestorian
						society_member_of = monastic_order_orthodox
						society_member_of = the_assassins
						society_member_of = the_cold_ones
						society_member_of = the_satanists
						society_member_of = monastic_order_stoics # Étudiant, Étudiante
					}
				}

				society_rank == 1
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = the_cult_of_kali
						society_member_of = the_plaguebringers
					}
				}

				OR = {
					society_rank == 1
					society_rank == 3
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { society_member_of = the_vodouns }

				OR = {
					society_rank == 1
					society_rank == 4
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # Héroïne
				society_rank == 4
				is_female = yes

				OR = {
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_norse
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_tengri
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_baltic
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_finnish
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_slavic
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_west_african
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_zun
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_bon
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_hellenic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_le_
		trigger = {
			is_female = no
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_la_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes
		}
	}
}

			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { society_member_of = hermetics }

				OR = {
					society_rank == 2
					society_rank == 3
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { society_member_of = monastic_order_buddhist }
				society_rank >= 3
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_hindu
						society_member_of = monastic_order_jain
					}
				}

				society_rank == 4
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = monastic_order_monophysite
						society_member_of = monastic_order_nestorian
						society_member_of = monastic_order_orthodox
						society_member_of = the_assassins
						society_member_of = the_cold_ones
						society_member_of = the_satanists
						society_member_of = monastic_order_stoics # Étudiant, Étudiante
					}
				}

				society_rank == 1
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						society_member_of = the_cult_of_kali
						society_member_of = the_plaguebringers
					}
				}

				OR = {
					society_rank == 1
					society_rank == 3
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { society_member_of = the_vodouns }

				OR = {
					society_rank == 1
					society_rank == 4
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # Héroïne
				society_rank == 4
				is_female = yes

				OR = {
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_norse
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_tengri
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_baltic
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_finnish
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_slavic
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_west_african
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_zun
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_bon
					society_member_of = warrior_lodge_hellenic
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
	}
}

				liege = {
					OR = {
						religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Darik-pat
						culture = greek # Sacellaire
						culture = han # Trésorier
						culture = jurchen # Trésorier
						culture = bodpa # Gnyer
						culture = tangut # Gnyer
						religion = taoist # Trésorier
						religion = aztec_pagan # Petlacalcatl
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }

				liege = {
					NOT = { religion_group = indian_group } # Upadhyaya

					trigger_if = {
						limit = { religion_group = muslim } # Imam de la Cour
						religion = shiite # Mollah de la Cour
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_job_title = job_spymaster
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
		trigger = {
			is_female = yes

			trigger_if = {
				limit = { has_job_title = job_chancellor }

				liege = {
					OR = {
						culture = bodpa # Lönchen
						culture = tangut # Lönchen
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else_if = {
				limit = { has_job_title = job_spiritual }

				liege = {
					OR = {
						religion_openly_norse_or_reformed_trigger = yes # Voyante
						culture = bodpa # Banchenmo
						culture = tangut # Banchenmo
					}
				}
			}
			trigger_else = {
				has_job_title = job_treasurer

				liege = {
					OR = {
						culture = bodpa # Gnyer
						culture = tangut # Gnyer
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_APOSTROPHE
		trigger = {
			trigger_if = { # femmes
				limit = { is_female = yes }

				has_job_title = job_spiritual

				liege = {
					religion_group = indian_group # Upadhyaya
				}
			}
			trigger_else = { # hommes
				trigger_if = {
					limit = { has_job_title = job_chancellor }

					liege = {
						religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Astabadh
					}
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { has_job_title = job_marshal }

					liege = {
						religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Eran Spahbod
					}
				}
				trigger_else_if = {
					limit = { has_job_title = job_treasurer }

					liege = {
						NOR = {
							religion_group = zoroastrian_group # Darik-pat
							culture = greek # Sacellaire
							culture = han # Trésorier
							culture = jurchen # Trésorier
							culture = bodpa # Gnyer
							culture = tangut # Gnyer
							religion = taoist # Trésorier
							religion = aztec_pagan # Petlacalcatl
						}
					}
				}
				trigger_else = {
					has_job_title = job_spiritual

					liege = {
						OR = {
							religion_group = indian_group # Upadhyaya

							trigger_if = {
								limit = { religion_group = muslim } # Imam de la Cour
								NOT = { religion = shiite } # Mollah de la Cour
							}
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_e_
	}
}

## HARDCODED ENGLISH COMMANDS WITH ARTICLE OR GENDER

defined_text = {
	name = GetReligiousGroupMascFem
	use_first_valid = yes

	text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_Random_GetReligiousGroupMascFem
		trigger = {
			has_alternate_start_parameter = {
				key = religion_names
				value = random
			}
		}
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = GetReligiousGroupMascKey
		trigger = { is_female = no }
	}
	text = {
		localisation_key = GetReligiousGroupFemKey
		trigger = { is_female = yes }
	}
	fallback_text = {
		localisation_key = String_FR_FALLBACK_GetReligiousGroupMascFem
	}
}

			lower_real_tier_than = KING
		}
